</p>
<ol><li>peas
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>стене́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:горох.html>горо́х</a></b> <i>or</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>сте́ну</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:стенка.html>сте́нку</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:горох.html>горо́х</a></b> <i>or</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>сте́ну</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:горох.html>горо́х</a></b> <i>or</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>стены́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:горох.html>горо́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak stené <b>goróx</b> <i>or</i> kak ob sténu/sténku <b>goróx</b> <i>or</i> kak v sténu <b>goróx</b> <i>or</i> kak ot stený <b>goróx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">like talking to a stone wall</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:горох.html>горо́хе</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pri caré Goróxe</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<i>jocular</i>) <i>in the days of yore</i></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> very small fruit, tubers, etc.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This is a collective noun. The singular <b><a href = vnd.unilang:горох.html>горо́х</a></b> corresponds to the plural in English. The plural <b><a href = vnd.unilang:горох.html>горо́хи</a></b> refers to different types of peas. A single pea is <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горошина.html>горо́шина</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">goróšina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pea, peas

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гороховый.html>горо́ховое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пюре.html>пюре́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>goróxovoje</b> pjurɛ́</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>pease</b> pudding</span></div></dd>

***горшок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:горшок.html>горшо́к</a> (4937)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a diminutive form of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gornъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(flower)pot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, out of which <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Macedonian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Macedonian language">Macedonian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="mk">грне</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grne</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ceramic pot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> comes. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">горщо́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">horщók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">горщо́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">horščók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горшок.html>горшо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">goršók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горшок.html>горшка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горшок.html>горшки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горшок.html>горшко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pot (a vessel)</li>
<li>flowerpot</li>
<li>chamber pot</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gorьkъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горький.html>го́рький</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">górʹkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)го́рче</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)го́рше</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">го́рший</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">горча́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bitter <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">comparative is <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">го́рче</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">górče</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>woeful, sorrowful <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">comparative is <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">го́рше</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">górše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">го́рший</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">góršij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unhappy, hopeless</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:горе.html>го́рь</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кий.html>кий</a></b>

Зализняка — 3*a/c'. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a>  |  <i>го́рче<span style="color:c0a300; cursor:help; font-size:x-small;" title="эта форма слова или ударение является нестандартной для данной схемы словоизменения"><sup>△</sup></span> (<a href = vnd.unilang:вкус.html>вкус</a>); го́рше<span style="color:c0a300; cursor:help; font-size:x-small;" title="эта форма слова или ударение является нестандартной для данной схемы словоизменения"><sup>△</sup></span>, го́рший<span style="color:c0a300; cursor:help; font-size:x-small;" title="эта форма слова или ударение является нестандартной для данной схемы словоизменения"><sup>△</sup></span> (<a href = vnd.unilang:эмоция.html>эмо́ция</a>)</i>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горький.html>го́рький</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">górʹkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горький.html>го́рько</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">górʹko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bitter, bitterly</li>
<li>poignant, poignantly</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горький.html>го́рько</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">górʹko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горький.html>го́рький</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">górʹkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горький.html>го́рько</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">górʹko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bitter! (<i>an old Russian tradition: a shout by wedding guests urging the newlyweds to kiss, thus removing the "bitterness"</i>)</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:горе.html>го́рь</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a>, определительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> предикатив, <a href = vnd.unilang:междометие.html>междоме́тие</a>; неизменяемое. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — горше.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-горьк-</b>; суффикс: <b>-о</b>.
</p>

***горячий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:горячий.html>горя́чий</a> (858)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">горѧчии</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">goręčii</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gorę</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gorěti</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to burn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́чий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jáčij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горящий.html>горя́щий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorjáščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горючий.html>горю́чий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorjúčij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горячий.html>горя́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gorjáčij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:горячий.html>горяче́е</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:горячий.html>горяче́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hot <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">having a high temperature</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>hot-tempered</li>
<li>heated</li>
<li>busy <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of time</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жаркий.html>жа́ркий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">žárkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жгучий.html>жгу́чий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">žgúčij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обжигающий.html>обжига́ющий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obžigájuščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>го<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ря́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чий</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a/b. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:горячий.html>горяче́е</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:горячий.html>горяче́й</a>, погоряче́е, погоряче́й.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-горяч-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">горячи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorjačítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горячиться.html>горячи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gorjačítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погорячиться.html>погорячи́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разгорячиться.html>разгорячи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get angry (and act or talk rashly), to fly into a passion, to lose one's temper</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">горячи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorjačítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">горячи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorjačítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горячка.html>горя́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gorjáčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горячка.html>горя́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горячка.html>горя́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горячка.html>горя́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fever (also figuratively); rush
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:горячка.html>горя́чка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bélaja <b>gorjáčka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">delirium tremens</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пороть.html>поро́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:горячка.html>горя́чку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">porótʹ <b>gorjáčku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dash about in a flap</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>го<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ря́ч<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-горяч-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смекалка.html>-к</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***горячность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:горячность.html>горя́чность</a> (16147)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горячий.html>горя́чий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorjáčij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горячность.html>горя́чность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gorjáčnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горячность.html>горя́чности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горячность.html>горя́чности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горячность.html>горя́чностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hot temper, hot-headed nature</li>
<li>fervor, ardor, zeal</li>
<li>vehemence</li></ol>
